Extract links if not already done\n        if (links.length === 0) {\n            $('a[href]').each((i, el) => {\n                const href = $(el).attr('href');\n                if (href && INSERT INTO crawl_queue (url, domain, depth, max_depth, parent_url, status, priority)\n                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, 'pending', 3)\n                    ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\n                `, [childUrl, new URL(childUrl).hostname, depth + 1, maxDepth, url]);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return {\n            success: true,\n            url,\n            title: * Parse a PDF file and extract products\n */\nasync function parsePDF(filePath, uploadedBy = { type: 'vendor', id: 'unknown' }) {\n    console.log(`[PDF] Parsing: ${filePath}`);\n    \n    // Create (original_filename, file_path, file_size_bytes, uploaded_by_type, uploaded_by_id, status, processing_started)\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, 'processing', NOW())\n        RETURNING id\n    `, totalPages) {\n    const products = [];\n    const lines = text.split('\\n').filter(l => l.trim().length > 0);\n    \n    let currentProduct = null;\n    let currentPage = 1;\n    const linesPerPage = Math.ceil(lines.length / totalPages);\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {\n        const line = lines[i].trim();\n        const page = Math.ceil((i + 1) / linesPerPage);\n        \n        // Skip very short lines or headers\n        if (line.length < 5) continue;\n        \n        // Detect potential product line (has price or SKU)\n        const hasPrice = PATTERNS.price.test(line);\n        PATTERNS.price.lastIndex = 0; // Reset regex\n        const hasSku = PATTERNS.sku.test(line);\n        PATTERNS.sku.lastIndex = 0;\n        \n        if (hasPrice || hasSku) {\n            // Extract price\n            const priceMatch = line.match(PATTERNS.price);\n            let price = null, currency = 'USD';\n            if (priceMatch) {\n                const priceStr = priceMatch[0];\n                if (priceStr.includes('\u20b9')) currency = 'INR';\n                else if (priceStr.includes('EUR')) currency = 'EUR';\n                else if (priceStr.includes('GBP')) currency = 'GBP';\n                price = parseFloat(priceStr.replace(/[^0-9.]/g, ''));\n            }\n            \n            // Extract SKU\n            PATTERNS.sku.lastIndex = 0;\n            const skuMatch = PATTERNS.sku.exec(line);\n            const sku = skuMatch ? skuMatch[1] : `VV-${Date.now()}-${products.length}`;\n            \n            // Extract dimensions\n            const dimMatches = [...line.matchAll(PATTERNS.dimensions)];\n            const dimensions = dimMatches.map(m => ({\n                width: parseFloat(m[1]),\n     const materials = [...new Set((line.match(PATTERNS.materials) || []).map(m => m.toLowerCase()))];\n            \n            // Extract colors\n            const colors = [...new const category = categoryMatch ? categoryMatch[0].toLowerCase() : 'general';\n            \n            // Build product name (first part of line before price/sku)\n            let name = line.split(/\\$|SKU|Item/i)[0].trim();\n            if (name.length < 3) name = `Product ${sku}`;\n            if (name.length > 200) name = name.substring(0, 200);\n            \n          unit: dimensions.length > 0 ?  SELECT * FROM email_queue \n        WHERE status = 'pending' AND attempts < 3\n        ORDER BY priority DESC, created_at ASC\n        LIMIT $1\n    `, [limit]);\n    \n    const results = [];\n `, [result.success ? \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udd22 Creating real embedding service...\"\n\ncat > \"$VV_HOME/backend/services/real-embeddings.cjs\" << 'EMBEDEOF'\n/**\n * VISTAVIEW REAL EMBEDDING SERVICE\n * Uses OpenAI ada-002 or local sentence-transformers\n */\n\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\nconst crypto = require('crypto');\n\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost', port: 5432 });\n\n// Configuration\nconst EMBEDDING_CONFIG = {\n    provider: process.env.EMBEDDING_PROVIDER || 'pseudo', // 'openai', 'local', 'pseudo'\n    openaiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY || '',\n    model: 'text-embedding-ada-002',\n    dimensions: 1536\n};\n\n/**\n * Generate embedding for text\n */\nasync function generateEmbedding(text) {\n    if (!text || text.trim().length === 0) {\n        return null;\n    }\n    \n    const cleanText = text.substring(0, 8000).trim(); // Limit for OpenAI\n    \n    switch (EMBEDDING_CONFIG.provider) {\n        case 'openai':\n            return generateOpenAIEmbedding(cleanText);\n        case 'local':\n            return generateLocalEmbedding(cleanText);\n        default:\n            return generatePseudoEmbedding(cleanText);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * OpenAI embedding\n */\nasync function generateOpenAIEmbedding(text) {\n    if (!EMBEDDING_CONFIG.openaiKey) {\n        console.log('[EMBED] No OpenAI key, falling back to pseudo');\n        return generatePseudoEmbedding(text);\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        const { OpenAI } = require('openai');\n        const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: EMBEDDING_CONFIG.openaiKey });\n        \n        const response = await openai.embeddings.create({\n            model: EMBEDDING_CONFIG.model,\n            input: text\n        });\n        \n        return response.data[0].embedding;\n    } catch (error) {\n        console.error('[EMBED] OpenAI error:', error.message);\n        return generatePseudoEmbedding(text);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Local embedding (placeholder for sentence-transformers)\n */\nasync function generateLocalEmbedding(text) {\n    // Would use something like:\n    // const { pipeline } = require('@xenova/transformers');\n    // const extractor = await pipeline('feature-extraction', 'Xenova/all-MiniLM-L6-v2');\n    console.log('[EMBED] Local embeddings not implemented, using pseudo');\n    return generatePseudoEmbedding(text);\n}\n\n/**\n * Pseudo embedding (deterministic, for testing)\n */\nfunction generatePseudoEmbedding(text) {\n    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha512').update(text).digest('hex');\n    const embedding = [];\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < EMBEDDING_CONFIG.dimensions; i++) {\n        const idx = i % 64;\n        const hexPair = hash.substring(idx * 2, idx * 2 + 2);\n        const value = (parseInt(hexPair, 16) / 255) * 2 - 1; // Normalize to [-1, 1]\n        embedding.push(value);\n    }\n    \n    // Normalize to unit vector\n    const magnitude = Math.sqrt(embedding.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v * v, 0));\n    return embedding.map(v => v / magnitude);\n}\n\n/**\n * Process embedding queue\n */\nasync function processEmbeddingQueue(limit = 50) {\n    console.log('[EMBED] Processing queue...');\n    \n    const pending = await pool.query(`\n        SELECT * FROM embedding_queue \n        WHERE status = 'pending'\n        ORDER BY created_at ASC\n        LIMIT $1\n    `, [limit]);\n    \n    let processed = 0, failed = 0;\n    \n    for (const item of pending.rows) {\n        try {\n            const embedding = await generateEmbedding(item.content_to_embed);\n            \n            if (embedding) {\n                // Update target table\n                const vectorStr = `[${embedding.join(',')}]`;\n                await pool.query(`\n                    UPDATE ${item.target_table} SET ${item.target_column} = $1::vector\n                    WHERE id = $2\n                `, [vectorStr, item.target_id]);\n                \n                await pool.query(`\n                    UPDATE embedding_queue SET status = 'completed', processed_at = NOW()\n                    WHERE id = $1\n                `, [item.id]);\n                \n                processed++;\n            } else {\n                throw new Error('Empty embedding');\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            await pool.query(`\n                UPDATE embedding_queue SET status = 'failed', error_message = $1\n                WHERE id = $2\n            `, [error.message, item.id]);\n            failed++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Update stats\n    await pool.query(`\n        UPDATE learning_stats SET embeddings_created = COALESCE(embeddings_created, 0) + $1, updated_at = NOW()\n        WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\n    `, [processed]);\n    \n    return { processed, failed, total: pending.rows.length };\n}\n\n/**\n * Queue item for embedding\n */\nasync function queueForEmbedding(targetTable, targetId, content, targetColumn = 'embedding') {\n    await pool.query(`\n        INSERT INTO embedding_queue (target_table, target_id, content_to_embed, target_column, status)\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, 'pending')\n        ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\n    `, [targetTable, targetId, content, targetColumn]);\n    \n    return { success: true, queued: true };\n}\n\n/**\n * Semantic search using embeddings\n */\nasync function semanticSearch(query, tableName, options = {}) {\n    const { limit = 10, minSimilarity = 0.5, column = 'embedding' } = options;\n    \n    const queryEmbedding = await generateEmbedding(query);\n    if (!queryEmbedding) return [];\n    \n    const vectorStr = `[${queryEmbedding.join(',')}]`;\n    \n    try {\n        const result = await pool.query(`\n            SELECT *, 1 - (${column} <=> $1::vector) as similarity\n            FROM ${tableName}\n            WHERE ${column} IS NOT NULL\n            ORDER BY ${column} <=> $1::vector\n            LIMIT $2\n        `, [vectorStr, limit]);\n        \n        return result.rows.filter(r => r.similarity >= minSimilarity);\n    } catch (error) {\n        console.error('[EMBED] Search error:', error.message);\n        return [];\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Find similar voice patterns\n */\nasync function findSimilarPatterns(text, limit = 5) {\n    return semanticSearch(text, 'crawled_voice_patterns', { limit });\n}\n\n/**\n * Find similar products\n */\nasync function findSimilarProducts(text, limit = 5) {\n    return semanticSearch(text, 'extracted_products', { limit });\n}\n\nmodule.exports = {\n    generateEmbedding,\n    processEmbeddingQueue,\n    queueForEmbedding,\n    semanticSearch,\n    findSimilarPatterns,\n    findSimilarProducts\n};\n\n// CLI execution\nif (require.main === module) {\n {\n        const embedding = await embeddings.generateEmbedding(text);\n        res.json({ success: true, dimensions: embedding?.length, embedding: embedding?.slice(0, 10) });\n    } catch (e) {\n 'CRAWLEREOF'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW REAL WEB CRAWLER\\n * Uses Puppeteer for JS-rendered pages, Cheerio for static pages\\n * Extracts voice patterns, commands, and UI text\\n */\\n\\nconst puppeteer = require('puppeteer');\\nconst cheerio = require('cheerio');\\nconst axios = require('axios');\\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\\n\\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost', port: 5432 });\\n\\n// Voice pattern detection regex\\nconst VOICE_PATTERNS = {\\n    commands: /\\\\b(say|tell|ask|play|open|show|navigate|go to|search for|find|create|add|remove|delete|update|save|send|call|text|email|schedule|set|turn on|turn off|start|stop|pause|resume|next|previous|skip|repeat|louder|quieter|mute|unmute)\\\\b/gi,\\n    queries: /\\\\b(what is|what's|how do|how to|where is|when is|who is|why is|can you|could you|would you|will you|is there|are there|do you|does it)\\\\b/gi,\\n    responses: /\\\\b(okay|ok|sure|yes|no|done|got it|understood|working on it|here you go|i found|i can|i cannot|sorry|thank you|you're welcome)\\\\b/gi,\\n    navigation: /\\\\b(home|back|forward|up|down|left|right|scroll|click|tap|swipe|zoom|close|exit|menu|settings|profile|dashboard)\\\\b/gi\\n};\\n\\n// Sites known for voice UI patterns\\nconst VOICE_UI_SITES = [\\n    { url: 'https://developer.amazon.com/en-US/docs/alexa/custom-skills/voice-interaction-model.html', domain: 'amazon', type: 'voice_assistant' },\\n    { url: 'https://developers.google.com/assistant/conversational/design', domain: 'google', type: 'voice_assistant' },\\n    { url: 'https://developer.apple.com/design/human-interface-guidelines/siri', domain: 'apple', type: 'voice_assistant' },\\n    { url: 'https://www.zillow.com/homes/', domain: 'zillow', type: 'real_estate' },\\n    { url: 'https://www.realtor.com/', domain: 'realtor', type: 'real_estate' },\\n    { url: 'https://www.homedepot.com/', domain: 'homedepot', type: 'home_improvement' },\\n    { url: 'https://www.lowes.com/', domain: 'lowes', type: 'home_improvement' }\\n];\\n\\n/**\\n * Crawl a single URL and extract content\\n */\\nasync function crawlUrl(url, options = {}) {\\n    const { useHeadless = true, depth = 0, maxDepth = 2, parentUrl = null } = options;\\n    \\n    console.log(`[CRAWLER] Crawling: ${url} (depth: ${depth})`);\\n    \\n    let browser = null;\\n    try {\\n        // Record in crawl_queue\\n        const queueResult = await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO crawl_queue (url, domain, depth, max_depth, parent_url, status, started_at)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, 'crawling', NOW())\\n            RETURNING id\\n        `, [url, new URL(url).hostname, depth, maxDepth, parentUrl]);\\n        const queueId = queueResult.rows[0].id;\\n        \\n        let html, pageTitle, links = [];\\n        \\n        // Try Puppeteer first for JS-rendered content\\n        try {\\n            browser = await puppeteer.launch({\\n                headless: useHeadless ? 'new' : false,\\n                args: ['--no-sandbox', '--disable-setuid-sandbox']\\n            });\\n            const page = await browser.newPage();\\n            await page.setUserAgent('VistaView-Crawler/1.0 (+https://vistaview.ai/bot)');\\n            await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'networkidle2', timeout: 30000 });\\n            \\n            html = await page.content();\\n            pageTitle = await page.title();\\n            \\n            // Extract all links\\n            links = await page.evaluate(() => {\\n                return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a[href]'))\\n                    .map(a => a.href)\\n                    .filter(href => href.startsWith('http'));\\n            });\\n            \\n            await browser.close();\\n            browser = null;\\n        } catch (puppeteerError) {\\n            console.log(`[CRAWLER] Puppeteer failed, trying axios: ${puppeteerError.message}`);\\n            // Fallback to axios for static pages\\n            const response = await axios.get(url, {\\n                timeout: 15000,\\n                headers: { 'User-Agent': 'VistaView-Crawler/1.0' }\\n            });\\n            html = response.data;\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Parse with Cheerio\\n        const $ = cheerio.load(html);\\n        pageTitle = pageTitle || $('title').text().trim();\\n        const metaDescription = $('meta[name=\\\"description\\\"]').attr('content') || '';\\n        \\n        // Extract text content\\n        $('script, style, noscript, iframe').remove();\\n        const textContent = $('body').text().replace(/\\\\s+/g, ' ').trim();\\n        \\n        // Extract voice patterns\\n        const extractedPatterns = extractVoicePatterns(textContent);\\n        \\n        // Extract links if not already done\\n        if (links.length === 0) {\\n            $('a[href]').each((i, el) => {\\n                const href = $(el).attr('href');\\n                if (href && href.startsWith('http')) links.push(href);\\n            });\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Update crawl_queue\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE crawl_queue SET \\n                status = 'completed',\\n                page_title = $1,\\n                meta_description = $2,\\n                extracted_content = $3,\\n                extracted_patterns = $4,\\n                discovered_links = $5,\\n                completed_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE id = $6\\n        `, [pageTitle, metaDescription, textContent.substring(0, 50000), extractedPatterns, links.slice(0, 100), queueId]);\\n        \\n        // Store patterns in crawled_voice_patterns\\n        const domain = new URL(url).hostname.replace('www.', '');\\n        for (const pattern of extractedPatterns) {\\n            await pool.query(`\\n                INSERT INTO crawled_voice_patterns (source_url, source_domain, source_type, pattern_text, pattern_type, pattern_category, confidence)\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, 'web_crawl', $3, $4, $5, 0.7)\\n                ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\\n            `, [url, domain, pattern.text, pattern.type, pattern.category]);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Update stats\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE learning_stats \\n            SET web_pages_crawled = web_pages_crawled + 1,\\n                patterns_learned = patterns_learned + $1,\\n                updated_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n        `, [extractedPatterns.length]);\\n        \\n        // Queue child links if depth allows\\n        if (depth < maxDepth) {\\n            const sameDomainLinks = links.filter(link => {\\n                try {\\n                    return new URL(link).hostname === new URL(url).hostname;\\n                } catch { return false; }\\n            }).slice(0, 10); // Limit to 10 child pages\\n            \\n            for (const childUrl of sameDomainLinks) {\\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    INSERT INTO crawl_queue (url, domain, depth, max_depth, parent_url, status, priority)\\n                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, 'pending', 3)\\n                    ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\\n                `, [childUrl, new URL(childUrl).hostname, depth + 1, maxDepth, url]);\\n            }\\n        }\\n        \\n        return {\\n            success: true,\\n            url,\\n            title: pageTitle,\\n            patternsFound: extractedPatterns.length,\\n            linksDiscovered: links.length,\\n            patterns: extractedPatterns\\n        };\\n        \\n    } catch (error) {\\n        console.error(`[CRAWLER] Error crawling ${url}:`, error.message);\\n        \\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE crawl_queue SET status = 'failed', error_message = $1, retry_count = retry_count + 1\\n            WHERE url = $2 AND status = 'crawling'\\n        `, [error.message, url]);\\n        \\n        return { success: false, url, error: error.message };\\n    } finally {\\n        if (browser) await browser.close();\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Extract voice patterns from text\\n */\\nfunction extractVoicePatterns(text) {\\n    const patterns = [];\\n    const seenPatterns = new Set();\\n    \\n    // Extract command patterns\\n    const commandMatches = text.match(VOICE_PATTERNS.commands) || [];\\n    for (const match of commandMatches) {\\n        const key = match.toLowerCase();\\n        if (!seenPatterns.has(key)) {\\n            seenPatterns.add(key);\\n            patterns.push({ text: match, type: 'command', category: 'action' });\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract query patterns\\n    const queryMatches = text.match(VOICE_PATTERNS.queries) || [];\\n    for (const match of queryMatches) {\\n        const key = match.toLowerCase();\\n        if (!seenPatterns.has(key)) {\\n            seenPatterns.add(key);\\n            patterns.push({ text: match, type: 'query', category: 'information' });\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract navigation patterns\\n    const navMatches = text.match(VOICE_PATTERNS.navigation) || [];\\n    for (const match of navMatches) {\\n        const key = match.toLowerCase();\\n        if (!seenPatterns.has(key)) {\\n            seenPatterns.add(key);\\n            patterns.push({ text: match, type: 'navigation', category: 'ui' });\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    return patterns.slice(0, 50); // Limit per page\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Process pending crawl queue\\n */\\nasync function processCrawlQueue(limit = 10) {\\n    console.log('[CRAWLER] Processing crawl queue...');\\n    \\n    const pending = await pool.query(`\\n        SELECT * FROM crawl_queue \\n        WHERE status = 'pending' AND retry_count < max_retries\\n        ORDER BY priority DESC, created_at ASC\\n        LIMIT $1\\n    `, [limit]);\\n    \\n    const results = [];\\n    for (const job of pending.rows) {\\n        const result = await crawlUrl(job.url, {\\n            depth: job.depth,\\n            maxDepth: job.max_depth,\\n            parentUrl: job.parent_url\\n        });\\n        results.push(result);\\n        \\n        // Small delay between requests\\n        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000));\\n    }\\n    \\n    return results;\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Start crawling voice UI sites\\n */\\nasync function crawlVoiceUISites() {\\n    console.log('[CRAWLER] Starting voice UI sites crawl...');\\n    \\n    // Create crawl job\\n    const job = await pool.query(`\\n        INSERT INTO crawl_jobs (job_type, target_url, target_domain, status, started_at)\\n        VALUES ('voice_patterns', 'multiple', 'voice_ui_sites', 'running', NOW())\\n        RETURNING id\\n    `);\\n    const jobId = job.rows[0].id;\\n    \\n    let totalPatterns = 0;\\n    let pagesProcessed = 0;\\n    \\n    for (const site of VOICE_UI_SITES) {\\n        // Queue the site\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO crawl_queue (url, domain, depth, max_depth, status, priority)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, 0, 2, 'pending', 10)\\n            ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\\n        `, [site.url, site.domain]);\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Process queue\\n    const results = await processCrawlQueue(VOICE_UI_SITES.length);\\n    \\n    for (const r of results) {\\n        if (r.success) {\\n            totalPatterns += r.patternsFound || 0;\\n            pagesProcessed++;\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Update job\\n    await pool.query(`\\n        UPDATE crawl_jobs SET \\n            status = 'completed',\\n            pages_crawled = $1,\\n            patterns_found = $2,\\n            completed_at = NOW()\\n        WHERE id = $3\\n    `, [pagesProcessed, totalPatterns, jobId]);\\n    \\n    return { jobId, pagesProcessed, totalPatterns };\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Add URL to crawl queue\\n */\\nasync function queueUrl(url, options = {}) {\\n    const { priority = 5, maxDepth = 2 } = options;\\n    try {\\n        const domain = new URL(url).hostname;\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO crawl_queue (url, domain, depth, max_depth, priority, status)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, 0, $3, $4, 'pending')\\n            ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\\n        `, [url, domain, maxDepth, priority]);\\n        return { success: true, url };\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        return { success: false, error: e.message };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nmodule.exports = {\\n    crawlUrl,\\n    processCrawlQueue,\\n    crawlVoiceUISites,\\n    queueUrl,\\n    extractVoicePatterns\\n};\\n\\n// CLI execution\\nif (require.main === module) {\\n    const args = process.argv.slice(2);\\n    if (args[0] === 'queue') {\\n        processCrawlQueue(parseInt(args[1]) || 10).then(r => {\\n            console.log('Results:', JSON.stringify(r, null, 2));\\n            process.exit(0);\\n        });\\n    } else if (args[0] === 'voice-sites') {\\n        crawlVoiceUISites().then(r => {\\n            console.log('Results:', JSON.stringify(r, null, 2));\\n            process.exit(0);\\n        });\\n    } else if (args[0]) {\\n        crawlUrl(args[0]).then(r => {\\n            console.log('Result:', JSON.stringify(r, null, 2));\\n            process.exit(0);\\n {\\n    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha512').update(text).digest('hex');\\n    const embedding = [];\\n    \\n    for (let i = 0; i < EMBEDDING_CONFIG.dimensions; i++) {\\n        const idx = i % 64;\\n        const hexPair = hash.substring(idx * 2, idx * 2 + 2);\\n        const value = (parseInt(hexPair, 16) / 255) * 2 - 1; // Normalize to [-1, 1]\\n        embedding.push(value);\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Normalize to unit vector\\n    const magnitude = Math.sqrt(embedding.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v * v, 0));\\n    return embedding.map(v => v / magnitude);\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Process embedding queue\\n */\\nasync function processEmbeddingQueue(limit = 50) {\\n    console.log('[EMBED] Processing queue...');\\n    \\n    const pending = await pool.query(`\\n        SELECT * FROM embedding_queue \\n        WHERE status = 'pending'\\n        ORDER BY created_at ASC\\n        LIMIT $1\\n    `, [limit]);\\n    \\n    let processed = 0, failed = 0;\\n    \\n    for (const item of pending.rows) {\\n        try {\\n            const embedding = await generateEmbedding(item.content_to_embed);\\n            \\n            if (embedding) {\\n                // Update target                  WHERE id = $2\\n                `, [vectorStr, item.target_id]);\\n                \\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    UPDATE embedding_queue SET status = embeddings_created = COALESCE(embeddings_created, 0) + $1, updated_at = NOW()\\n        WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n    `, [processed]);\\n    \\n    return { processed, failed, total: pending.rows.length };\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Queue item for embedding\\n */\\nasync function queueForEmbedding(targetTable, targetId, content, targetColumn = 'embedding') {\\n    await pool.query(`\\n        INSERT INTO embedding_queue (target_table, target_id, content_to_embed, target_column, status)\\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, 'pending')\\n        ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING\\n    `, [targetTable, targetId, content, targetColumn]);\\n    \\n    return { success: true, queued: true };\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Semantic search using embeddings\\n */\\nasync function semanticSearch(query, tableName, options = {}) {\\n    const { limit = 10, minSimilarity = 0.5, column = 'embedding' } = options;\\n    \\n    const queryEmbedding = await generateEmbedding(query);\\n    if (!queryEmbedding) return [];\\n    \\n    const vectorStr = `[${queryEmbedding.join(',')}]`;\\n    \\n    try {\\n        const result = await pool.query(`\\n            SELECT *, 1 - (${column} <=> $1::vector) as similarity\\n            FROM ${tableName}\\n            WHERE ${column} IS NOT NULL\\n            ORDER BY ${column} <=> $1::vector\\n            LIMIT $2\\n        `, [vectorStr, limit]);\\n        \\n        return result.rows.filter(r => r.similarity >= minSimilarity);\\n    } catch (error) {\\n        console.error('[EMBED] Search error:', error.message);\\n        return [];\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Find similar voice patterns\\n */\\nasync function findSimilarPatterns(text, limit = 5) {\\n    return semanticSearch(text, 'crawled_voice_patterns', { limit });\\n}\\n\\n/**\\n * Find similar products\\n */\\nasync function findSimilarProducts(text, limit = 5) {\\n    return semanticSearch(text, 'extracted_products', { limit });\\n}\\n\\nmodule.exports = {\\n    generateEmbedding,\\n    processEmbeddingQueue,\\n    queueForEmbedding,\\n    semanticSearch,\\n    findSimilarPatterns,\\n    findSimilarProducts\\n};\\n\\n// CLI execution\\nif (require.main === module) {\\n    const args = process.argv.slice(2);\\n    if (args[0] === 'process') {\\n        processEmbeddingQueue(parseInt(args[1]) || 50).then(r => {\\n            console.log('Result:', JSON.stringify(r, null, 2));\\n            process.exit(0);\\n        });\\n    } else if (args[0] === 'search') {\\n        semanticSearch(args.slice(1).join(' '), 'crawled_voice_patterns').then(r => {\\n            console.log('Results:', JSON.stringify(r, null, 2));\\n            process.exit(0);\\n        });\\n    } else if (args[0]) {\\n        generateEmbedding(args.join(' ')).then(r => {\\n            console.log('Embedding length:', r?.length);\\n            console.log('First 5 values:', r?.slice(0, 5));\\n            process.exit(0);\\n        });\\n    } else {\\n        console.log('Usage: node real-embeddings.cjs <text>');\\n        console.log('       node real-embeddings.cjs process [limit]');\\n        console.log('       node real-embeddings.cjs search <query>');\\n    }\\n}\\nEMBEDEOF\\n\\necho \\\"\\u2705 Real embedding service \"$VV_HOME/frontend/src/components/agentic/AgenticBar.jsx\" << 'AGENTICEOF'\n/**\n * VISTAVIEW AGENTIC BAR - React Component\n * Global voice interface that appears on every page\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { useAgentic } from '../../context/AgenticContext';\nimport { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';\nimport './AgenticBar.css';\n\nconst AgenticBar = () => {\n    const navigate = useNavigate();\n    const location = useLocation();\n    const { \n        sessionId, \n        userType, \n        setUserType,\n        sendVoice, \n        lastResponse, \n        isConnected,\n        navStack,\n        goBack,\n        goHome\n    } = useAgentic();\n    \n    const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n    const [interimTranscript, setInterimTranscript] = useState('');\n    const [badges, setBadges] = useState([]);\n    const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);\n    const recognitionRef = useRef(null);\n    const synthRef = useRef(window.speechSynthesis);\n    \n    // Initialize speech recognition\n    useEffect(() => {\n        if ('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window || 'SpeechRecognition' in window) {\n            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;\n            recognitionRef.current = new SpeechRecognition();\n            recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n            recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n            recognitionRef.current.lang = 'en-US';\n            \n            recognitionRef.current.onresult = handleSpeechResult;\n            recognitionRef.current.onerror = handleSpeechError;\n            recognitionRef.current.onend = () => {\n                if (isListening) recognitionRef.current.start();\n            };\n        }\n        \n        return () => {\n            if (recognitionRef.current) recognitionRef.current.stop();\n        };\n    }, [isListening]);\n    \n    // Handle speech result\n    const handleSpeechResult = useCallback(async (event) => {\n        let final = '';\n        let interim = '';\n        \n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n            if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\n                final += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n            } else {\n                interim += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        setInterimTranscript(interim);\n        \n        if (final) {\n            setTranscript(final);\n            await processVoiceInput(final);\n        }\n    }, []);\n    \n    const handleSpeechError = (event) => {\n        if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {\n            console.error('Speech error:', event.error);\n            stopListening();\n        }\n    };\n    \n    // Process voice input\n    const processVoiceInput = async (text) => {\n        const response = await sendVoice(text, location.pathname);\n        \n        if (response?.analysis) {\n            const a = response.analysis;\n            setBadges([\n                { text: a.sentiment, type: a.sentiment },\n                { text: a.emotion, type: 'emotion' },\n                { text: a.intent, type: 'intent' },\n                { text: `${Math.round(a.empathyScore * 100)}%`, type: 'empathy' }\n            ]);\n            \n            // Handle navigation intents\n            if (a.intent === 'system_back') {\n                goBack();\n            } else if (a.intent === 'system_close' || a.intent === 'system_home') {\n                goHome();\n            } else if (a.intent === 'navigation') {\n                handleNavigation(text);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Speak TTS response\n        if (response?.tts_response?.text) {\n            speak(response.tts_response.text);\n        }\n    };\n    \n    // Handle navigation commands\n    const handleNavigation = (text) => {\n        const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n        \n        if (lower.includes('dashboard')) navigate('/dashboard');\n        else if (lower.includes('home')) navigate('/');\n        else if (lower.includes('products') || lower.includes('catalog')) navigate('/products');\n        else if (lower.includes('vendors')) navigate('/vendors');\n        else if (lower.includes('properties')) navigate('/properties');\n        else if (lower.includes('settings')) navigate('/settings');\n        else if (lower.includes('profile')) navigate('/profile');\n    };\n    \n    // TTS\n    const speak = (text) => {\n        synthRef.current.cancel();\n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n        utterance.rate = 1.0;\n        utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n    };\n    \n    // Toggle listening\n    const toggleListening = () => {\n        if (isListening) {\n            stopListening();\n        } else {\n            startListening();\n        }\n    };\n    \n    const startListening = () => {\n        if (recognitionRef.current) {\n            setTranscript('');\n            setInterimTranscript('');\n            recognitionRef.current.start();\n            setIsListening(true);\n        }\n    };\n    \n    const stopListening = () => {\n        if (recognitionRef.current) {\n            recognitionRef.current.stop();\n        }\n        setIsListening(false);\n    };\n    \n    return (\n        <div className={`agentic-bar ${isExpanded ? 'expanded' : ''}`}>\n            <div className=\"agentic-bar-main\">\n                <button \n                    className={`mic-button ${isListening ? 'listening' : ''}`}\n                    onClick={toggleListening}\n                    title={isListening ? 'Stop listening' : 'Start listening'}\n                >\n                    {isListening ? '\ud83d\udd34' : '\ud83c\udfa4'}\n                </button>\n                \n                <div className=\"agentic-bar-content\">\n                    <div className=\"agentic-bar-header\">\n                        <span className=\"agentic-bar-title\">\ud83e\udd16 Mr. V</span>\n                        <select \n                            className=\"user-type-select\"\n                            value={userType}\n                            onChange={(e) => setUserType(e.target.value)}\n                        >\n                            <option value=\"boss\">\ud83d\udc64 Boss</option>\n                            <option value=\"dev_team\">\ud83d\udc65 Dev Team</option>\n                            <option value=\"vendor\">\ud83c\udfea Vendor</option>\n                            <option value=\"builder\">\ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f Builder</option>\n                            <option value=\"buyer\">\ud83c\udfe0 Buyer</option>\n                            <option value=\"visitor\">\ud83d\udc41\ufe0f Visitor</option>\n                        </select>\n                        <span className={`connection-status ${isConnected ? 'connected' : ''}`}>\n                            {isConnected ? '\u25cf' : '\u25cb'}\n                        </span>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    <div className=\"transcript-area\">\n                        {isListening ? (\n                            <span className=\"interim\">{interimTranscript || 'Listening...'}</span>\n                        ) : (\n                            <span>{transcript || 'Click mic to speak'}</span>\n                        )}\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    {badges.length > 0 && (\n                        <div className=\"badges\">\n                            {badges.map((badge, i) => (\n                                <span key={i} className={`badge badge-${badge.type}`}>\n                                    {badge.text}\n                                </span>\n                            ))}\n                        </div>\n                    )}\n                </div>\n                \n                <div className=\"agentic-bar-actions\">\n                    <button onClick={goBack} title=\"Go Back\" disabled={navStack.length <= 1}>\n                        \u25c0\n                    </button>\n                    <button onClick={goHome} title=\"Go Home\">\n                        \ud83c\udfe0\n                    </button>\n                    <button onClick={() => setIsExpanded(!isExpanded)} title=\"Expand\">\n                        {isExpanded ? '\u25bc' : '\u25b2'}\n                    </button>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            {isExpanded && (\n                <div className=\"agentic-bar-expanded\">\n                    <div className=\"nav-stack\">\n                        <strong>Navigation History:</strong>\n                        {navStack.slice(-5).map((item, i) => (\n                            <span key={i} className=\"nav-item\">{item.title || item.route}</span>\n                        ))}\n                    </div>\n                    <div className=\"quick-actions\">\n                        <button onClick={() => navigate('/dashboard')}>\ud83d\udcca Dashboard</button>\n                        <button onClick={() => navigate('/products')}>\ud83d\udce6 Products</button>\n                        <button onClick={() => navigate('/properties')}>\ud83c\udfe0 Properties</button>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            )}\n        </div>\n    );\n};\n\nexport {\n    const navigate = useNavigate();\n    const location = useLocation();\n    \n    const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState(null);\n    const [userType, setUserType] = useState('visitor');\n    const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState(false);\n    const [lastResponse, setLastResponse] = useState(null);\n    const [navStack, setNavStack] = useState([]);\n    const [feed, setFeed] = wsRef.current.close();\n        };\n    }, []);\n    \n    // Track navigation\n    useEffect(() => {\n        pushNavigation(location.pathname, document.title);\n    }, [location.pathname]);\n    \n    const initSession = async () => {\n        try {\n            const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/session/start`, {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    user_type: userType,\n                    device_type: navigator.userAgent.includes('Mobile') ? 'mobile' : 'desktop',\n                    browser: navigator.userAgent\n                })\n            });\n            const data = await res.json();\n            if (data.session_id) {\n                setSessionId(data.session_id);\n                setIsConnected(true);\n                initWebSocket(data.session_id);\n            }\n        } catch (e) {\n            console.error('Session init error:', e);\n        }\n    };\n    \n    const initWebSocket = (sid) => {\n        try {\n            const ws = new WebSocket(`ws://localhost:1117/ws?session=${sid}`);\n            ws.onmessage = (event) => {\n                const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                if (data.type === 'feed') {\n                    setFeed(prev => [data.item, ...prev].slice(0, 50));\n                }\n            };\n            ws.onclose = () => setIsConnected(false);\n            ws.onerror = () => console.log('WebSocket not available');\n            wsRef.current = ws;\n        } catch (e) {\n            // WebSocket not available\n        }\n    };\n    \n    const sendVoice = useCallback(async (text, pageRoute = location.pathname) => {\n        try {\n            const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/ledger/log`, {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    user_type: userType,\n                    session_id: sessionId,\n                    raw_transcript: text,\n                    page_route: pageRoute,\n                    interaction_mode: 'voice'\n                })\n            });\n            const data = await res.json();\n            setLastResponse(data);\n            return data;\n        } catch (e) {\n            console.error('Voice send error:', e);\n            return null;\n        }\n    }, [sessionId, userType, location.pathname]);\n    \n    const pushNavigation = useCallback(async (route, title) => {\n        if (!sessionId) return;\n        \n        setNavStack(prev => [...prev, { route, title, timestamp: Date.now() }]);\n        \n        try {\n            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/navigation/push`, {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    session_id: sessionId,\n                    page_route: route,\n                    page_title: title\n                })\n            });\n        } catch (e) {}\n    }, [sessionId]);\n    \n    const goBack = useCallback(async () => {\n        if (navStack.length > 1) {\n            try {\n                const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/navigation/back`, {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId })\n                });\n                const data = await res.json();\n                if (data.success && data.page) {\n                    setNavStack(prev => prev.slice(0, -1));\n                    navigate(data.page.page_route);\n                }\n            } catch (e) {\n                navigate(-1);\n            }\n        }\n    }, [sessionId, navStack, navigate]);\n    \n    const goHome = useCallback(async () => {\n        try {\n            await fetch(`${API_BASE}/navigation/home`, {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId })\n            });\n        } catch (e) {}\n        setNavStack([]);\n        navigate('/');\n    }, [sessionId, navigate]);\n    \n    const value = {\n        sessionId,\n        userType,\n        setUserType,\n        isConnected,\n        lastResponse,\n        navStack,\n        feed,\n        sendVoice,\n        goBack,\n        goHome,\n        pushNavigation,\n        API_BASE\n    };\n    \n    return (\n        <AgenticContext.Provider value={value}>\n            {children}\n        </AgenticContext.Provider>\n    );\n};\n\nexport const useAgentic = () => {\n    const context = useContext(AgenticContext);\n    if (!context) {\n        throw new Error('useAgentic must be used within AgenticProvider');\n    }\n    return context;\n};\n\nexport default error:', event.error);\\n            stopListening();\\n        }\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Process voice input\\n    const processVoiceInput = async (text) => {\\n        const response = await a.sentiment },\\n                { text: a.emotion, type: 'emotion' },\\n                { text: a.intent, type: 'intent' },\\n                { text: `${Math.round(a.empathyScore * 100)}%`, type: 'empathy' }\\n            ]);\\n            \\n            // Handle navigation intents\\n            if (a.intent === 'system_back') {\\n                goBack();\\n            } else if (a.intent commands\\n    const handleNavigation = (text) => {\\n        const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n        \\n        if (lower.includes('dashboard')) navigate('/dashboard');\\n        else if (lower.includes('home')) navigate('/');\\n        else if (lower.includes('products') || lower.includes('catalog')) navigate('/products');\\n        else if (lower.includes('vendors')) navigate('/vendors');\\n        else if (lower.includes('properties')) navigate('/properties');\\n        else if (lower.includes('settings')) navigate('/settings');\\n        else if (lower.includes('profile')) navigate('/profile');\\n    };\\n    \\n    // TTS\\n    const speak = (text) => {\\n        synthRef.current.cancel();\\n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n        utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n        utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n        synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Toggle listening\\n    const toggleListening = () => {\\n        if (isListening) {\\n            stopListening();\\n        } else {\\n            startListening();\\n        }\\n    };\\n    \\n    const startListening = () => {\\n        if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n            setTranscript('');\\n            setInterimTranscript('');\\n            recognitionRef.current.start();\\n            setIsListening(true);\\n        }\\n    };\\n    \\n    const stopListening = () => {\\n        if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n            recognitionRef.current.stop();\\n        }\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n    };\\n    \\n    return (\\n        <div className={`agentic-bar ${isExpanded ? 'expanded' : ''}`}>\\n            <div className=\\\"agentic-bar-main\\\">\\n                <button \\n                    className={`mic-button ${isListening ?
